PO RGYAL DBANG THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG RGYA MTSO DPAL BZANG PO'O, ,DBEN PA'I RI 

SUL DU SGRUB PA SNYING POR MDZAD PA'I SGO NAS 'PHRIN LAS RGYA CHER SPEL BAR MDZAD PA NI SRAS KYI THU BO GRUB 

PA'I DBANG PHYUG BRTZON 'GRUS RGYAL MTSAN, GU GE CHOS RJE SNYING STOBS RGYA MTSO, RJE NYID KYI RGYAL TSAB TU BKRA 

SHIS LHUN PO'I RGYU DPA GRVA TSANG GI GDAN SAR MNGA' GSOL BA RDO RJE 'DZIN PA DKON MCHOG RGYAL MTSAN,

GRUB PA'I DBANG PHYUG GNAS BCU RAB 'BYAMS PA DGE 'DUN RGYAL MTSAN, SNYAN RGYUD 'PHRIN LAS KYI BKA' 

BAB DRUNG BA LTA PHUG PA DAM CHOS RGYAL MTSAN, ZHABS DRUNG LHA PA BLO BZANG BSTAN PA DAR RGYAS, DBANG 

RJES GNANG GI 'PHRIN LAS KYI BKA' BAB SKYID SHOD ZHABS DRUNG NGAG DBANG BSTAN 'DZIN 'PHRIN LAS, ZAB 

DON LTA BA'I BKA' BAB DKA' CHEN NAM MKHA' RDO RJE, DBANG PHYUG GI STOBS KYIS BSTAN PA SKYONG BA'I BKA' 

BAB SE CHEN CHOS RJE SOGS NYI ZLA LTAR YONGS SU GRAGS PA'I BSTAN 'DZIN DAM PA'ANG CHES MANG NGO,,
